***agressie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:agressie.html>agressie</a> (7958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">agression</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">aggressiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:agressie.html>agressie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:agressies.html>agressies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:agressie.html>agressietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hostile, aggressive behaviour, aggression</li>
<li>aggression, the act of initiating hostile activities, e.g. a military invasion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> attack</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ah.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a> (1980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>mid-1400s Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> (replacing <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">la</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">An expression of relief, relaxation, comfort, confusion, understanding, wonder, awe, etc. <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to uttered inflection.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a></b>, I understand now.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a></b>! It's good to be back home!</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a></b>, the flowers of spring.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">A syllable used to fill space, particularly in music.</span>
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, Britney Spears, <i>Womanizer</i> (song)
<dl><dd>Boy don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> try to front, <a href = vnd.unilang:uh.html>uh</a>, I<br />Know just, just, what you are, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ahs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instance of the interjection <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></i>.
<dl><dd><i>the crowd's oohs and <b>ahs</b> at the fireworks</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ahs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ahing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ahed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To give a cry of "<a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a>".
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Rhoads, <i>Sinner, Sailor: A Memoir</i> (page 221)
<dl><dd>Mother and dad oohed and <b>ahed</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Cindy. She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> only two months old but already <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> developing her personality.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>ah</a></strong> (<i>personal pronoun</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a></b>, <i>possessive adjective</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">mah</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Eye dialect spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">I</i></span></span>., most often indicating that the speaker <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> using a Scottish or American (particularly Southern) <a href = vnd.unilang:accent.html>accent</a>.</span></li></ol>

***ahoy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a> (23590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From "a-hoy"; 'hoy' being a Middle English greeting <a href = vnd.unilang:dating.html>dating</a> back to the fourteenth century.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Used to hail a ship, a boat or a person, or to attract attention.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1751</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tobias_Smollett" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tobias Smollett">Tobias Smollett</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Adventures_of_Peregrine_Pickle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Adventures of Peregrine Pickle">The Adventures of Peregrine Pickle</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> thus occupied, a voice, still more uncouth than the former, bawled <a href = vnd.unilang:aloud.html>aloud</a>, ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>Ho</a>! the house, a-hoy!’</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 7, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I made a speaking trumpet of my hands and commenced to whoop “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>Ahoy</a>!</b>” and “Hello!” at the top of my lungs. […] The Colonel woke up, and, after asking what in <a href = vnd.unilang:brimstone.html>brimstone</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the matter, opened his mouth and roared “Hi!” and “Hello!” like the bull of Bashan.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Warning of something approaching or impending.
<ul><li><b>1989</b>, <i>Forbes</i> (volume 143, issues 5-7, page 74)
<dl><dd>Lawsuits, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a></b>! <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:towns.html>Towns</a> can regulate use of their <a href = vnd.unilang:beaches.html>beaches</a>. But what about the waters offshore?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1992</b>, <i>Championship Run</i> (video game review) in <i>Your Sinclair</i> issue 75, page 61
<dl><dd>Catalytic converters <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a></b> – Zeppelin's latest <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of those high-rev 3D driving games that simulates racing <a href = vnd.unilang:tracks.html>tracks</a> from all <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the world.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Traditionally, when used from a ship to hail an approaching boat, the standard responses are:
<ul><li>"<a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aye.html>aye</a>", if a commissioned officer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the boat;</li>
<li>"no no", if no officer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the boat;</li>
<li><i>name of ship</i>, if the <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>captain</a> of another ship <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the boat;</li>
<li>"flag" if an admiral <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in the boat.</li></ul></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to attract attention</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oi.html>oi</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yo.html>yo</a></span>; see also Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>hey</a></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ahoys</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ahoying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ahoyed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To hail with a cry of "<a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a>".</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ahoy.html>ahoy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ahoys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An utterance of this interjection.
<dl><dd><i>There <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> many <b>ahoys</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> from the approaching ship.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eiche</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eik.html>eik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">oak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href = vnd.unilang:eik.html>eik</a></i>.

***ais.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ais.html>ais</a> (18492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">īs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">īs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*īsą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:eis.html>Eis</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijs.html>ijs</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ice</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">ís</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="cim"><a href = vnd.unilang:ais.html>ais</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luserna" class="extiw" title="w:Luserna">Luserna</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sette_Comuni" class="extiw" title="w:Sette Comuni">Sette Comuni</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thirteen_Communities" class="extiw" title="w:Thirteen Communities">Thirteen Communities</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="cim">'Z <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ais.html>ais</a></b> ist bassar gabróart.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Ice</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> frozen water. <span style="font-size:85%;">(Sette Comuni dialect)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***aitch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aitch.html>aitch</a> (55159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ache</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ache</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*acca</i>, probably an extension of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a></i>, from an unindentified source. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">acca</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:aitch.html>aitch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">aitches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">The name of the Latin-script letter <span class="mention">H</span>.</span>
<ul><li><b>1773</b>, <i>The Monthly Review Or Literary Journal Enlarged</i>, October
<dl><dd>The word length, which contains only four <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> l e ng th, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually spell'd thus, el ee <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> gee tee <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aitch.html>aitch</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H.G._Wells" class="extiw" title="w:H.G. Wells">H.G. Wells</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_War_of_the_Worlds" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The War of the Worlds">The War of the Worlds</a></cite>, London |  William Heinemann, page 257:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"If you've got any drawing-room manners, or a dislike to eating peas with a knife or <a href = vnd.unilang:dropping.html>dropping</a> <b>aitches</b>, you'd better <a href = vnd.unilang:chuck.html>chuck</a> 'em away. They ain'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> no further use."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1959</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Burgess" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Anthony Burgess">Anthony Burgess</a>,  <cite>Beds in the East</cite> (The Malayan Trilogy), published 1972, page 469:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She frowned, hearing <a href = vnd.unilang:lim.html>Lim</a> Cheng Po's voice, so English, so refined, so very English upper-class. And often she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to tell <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a> about his <b>aitches</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>The word hour <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written with a silent <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aitch.html>aitch</a></b>.</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:cockneys.html>Cockneys</a> drop their <b>aitches</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ajuin.html>ajuin</a> (77443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oinjun</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ayuun</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ejuun</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">oignon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">onion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ui</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">onion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rams.html>rams</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ramson; now only in place names</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:acte.html>acte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:acte.html>acte</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aktief.html>aktief</a> (95854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aktief.html>aktief</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aktiever.html>aktiever</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">aktiefst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Superseded spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actief.html>actief</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>

<ul><li>The spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aktief.html>aktief</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> deprecated in 1996 in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_Dutch_orthographyThe_spelling_reform_of_1996_(The_Netherlands_and_Flanders)" class="extiw" title="w:History of Dutch orthography">the new <i><a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>Groene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boekje.html>Boekje</a></i> (“Little Green Book”) spelling reform</a>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***al.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> (70)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*allaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>all, all of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdrinken.html>opgedronken</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> you <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> <b>all</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Gogh <a href = vnd.unilang:produceerde.html>produceerde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:periode.html>periode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slechts.html>slechts</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tien.html>tien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Gogh produced <b>all of</b> his work during a period of only ten years.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tanker <a href = vnd.unilang:gelekt.html>gelekt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>All the</b> oil <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> leaked out of the tanker.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a> (1801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">all' <a href = vnd.unilang:arme.html>arme</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to arms</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">allarme</i>; cf. also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">alarme</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alarmen.html>alarmen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarmpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***alarmeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alarmeren.html>alarmeren</a> (23930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">alarmer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alarmeren.html>alarmeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a>, bring in a state of alert, warn, notably by means of an <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a> signal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitkijkposten.html>uitkijkposten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:alarmeren.html>alarmeren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdkwartier.html>hoofdkwartier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:telkens.html>telkens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijand.html>vijand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadert.html>nadert</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The observer <a href = vnd.unilang:posts.html>posts</a> <b>alert</b> HQ each time the enemy approaches.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:alarm.html>alarm</a>, disquiet, disturb</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:albus.html>albus</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a>'tje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a></span>: person or animal congenitally lacking melanin pigmentation in the skin, <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>, and hair or <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> (or more rarely only in the <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>); one afflicted with albinism</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:albino.html>albino</a></span>, albinistic: congenitally lacking melanin pigmentation in the skin, <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>, and hair or <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> (or more rarely only in the <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>); afflicted with albinism</li></ol>

lang="grc">χημεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khēmeía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χυμεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khumeía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> originally “a mingling, infusion, juice, liquid, as extracted from gold” and <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> “alchemie”, perhaps from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Χημία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Khēmía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black earth (ancient name for Egypt)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and/or <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χυμός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khumós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">juice, <a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. (Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">alquimia</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">alchimia</i>).
</p>
